***иной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a> (439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)inъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>other, another, different</li>
<li>some, many a
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">inój raz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sometimes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne kto <b>inój</b>, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nobody else but</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́е</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne što <b>inóje</b>, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nothing else but</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рка</a> (12243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:марка.html>ма́рка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inostránnaja márka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; since the 1980s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inomárka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рок</a></b>)

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>Одна́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кафедра.html>ка́федру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подозрительный.html>подозри́тельного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщить.html>сообщи́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:инопланетянин.html>инопланетя́нин</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основание.html>основа́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребовать.html>потре́бовал</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропустить.html>пропусти́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заседание.html>заседа́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кафедра.html>ка́федры</a>. </span></li>

***инородец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дец</a> (30185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инородный.html>иноро́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inoródnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inoródec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Non-Russian <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the designation of minority nations in imperial Russia; usually of nomadic peoples of the East, such as Buryats, Kalmyks, Kirghiz, Yakuts, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инстинктивный.html>инстинкти́вный</a> (8800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">instinktiv</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инстинктивный.html>инстинкти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">instinktívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)инстинкти́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)инстинкти́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>instinctive</li>
<li>involuntary, unconscious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:инстинктивный.html>инстинкти́вное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>instinktívnoje</b> dvižénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">involuntary movement</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инструментальный.html>инструмента́льный</a> (18105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инструмент.html>инструме́нт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">instrumént</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-álʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инструментальный.html>инструмента́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">instrumentálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> instrumental</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tool, toolmaking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:инструментальный.html>инструмента́льное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>instrumentálʹnoje</b> proizvódstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tool production</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:инструментальный.html>инструмента́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кладовая.html>кладова́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>instrumentálʹnaja</b> kladovája</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tool crib</span></div></dd>

***инсценировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инсценировать.html>инсцени́ровать</a> (29780)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">inszenieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">in Szene</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in scene</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инсценировать.html>инсцени́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inscenírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to adapt (a literary work) for theater, to film or television; to stage (a literary work)</li></ol>
